\begin{SaveVerbatim}{HOLPlanPBDefDefinitionssecContextXXdef}
\HOLTokenTurnstile{} \HOLSymConst{\HOLTokenForall{}}\HOLBoundVar{s} \HOLBoundVar{x}.
     \HOLConst{secContext} \HOLBoundVar{s} \HOLBoundVar{x} \HOLSymConst{=}
     \HOLKeyword{if} \HOLBoundVar{s} \HOLSymConst{=} \HOLConst{WARNO} \HOLKeyword{then}
       \HOLKeyword{if}
         (\HOLConst{getRecon} \HOLBoundVar{x} \HOLSymConst{=} [\HOLConst{SOME} (\HOLConst{SLc} (\HOLConst{PL} \HOLConst{recon}))]) \HOLSymConst{\HOLTokenConj{}}
         (\HOLConst{getTenativePlan} \HOLBoundVar{x} \HOLSymConst{=} [\HOLConst{SOME} (\HOLConst{SLc} (\HOLConst{PL} \HOLConst{tentativePlan}))]) \HOLSymConst{\HOLTokenConj{}}
         (\HOLConst{getReport} \HOLBoundVar{x} \HOLSymConst{=} [\HOLConst{SOME} (\HOLConst{SLc} (\HOLConst{PL} \HOLConst{report1}))]) \HOLSymConst{\HOLTokenConj{}}
         (\HOLConst{getInitMove} \HOLBoundVar{x} \HOLSymConst{=} [\HOLConst{SOME} (\HOLConst{SLc} (\HOLConst{PSG} \HOLConst{initiateMovement}))])
       \HOLKeyword{then}
         [\HOLConst{PL_WARNO_Auth};
          \HOLConst{Name} \HOLConst{PlatoonLeader} \HOLConst{controls}
          \HOLConst{prop} (\HOLConst{SOME} (\HOLConst{SLc} (\HOLConst{PL} \HOLConst{recon})));
          \HOLConst{Name} \HOLConst{PlatoonLeader} \HOLConst{controls}
          \HOLConst{prop} (\HOLConst{SOME} (\HOLConst{SLc} (\HOLConst{PL} \HOLConst{tentativePlan})));
          \HOLConst{Name} \HOLConst{PlatoonSergeant} \HOLConst{controls}
          \HOLConst{prop} (\HOLConst{SOME} (\HOLConst{SLc} (\HOLConst{PSG} \HOLConst{initiateMovement})))]
       \HOLKeyword{else} [\HOLConst{prop} \HOLConst{NONE}]
     \HOLKeyword{else} \HOLKeyword{if} \HOLConst{getPlCom} \HOLBoundVar{x} \HOLSymConst{=} \HOLConst{invalidPlCommand} \HOLKeyword{then} [\HOLConst{prop} \HOLConst{NONE}]
     \HOLKeyword{else} [\HOLConst{PL_notWARNO_Auth} (\HOLConst{getPlCom} \HOLBoundVar{x})]
\end{SaveVerbatim}
